<Review>Great location, outdoor seating is tree lined next to a small grassy park, a pleasant surprise amidst the surrounding industrial buildings. Walking up I was not sure if I was at the right location as it is in an industrial location. Once Inside I was greeted by friendly and professional staff. I was greeted not only by the cashier but a few individuals behind the counter. My cashier Janyne was extremely kind, helpful and professional. Her suggestion on the Ginger Chicken soup was just what I was looking for on the cool overcast So Cal afternoon, warmed me right up. Loaded with fresh dark and white meat chicken and rice with just the right kick of ginger. Quick to point out the best deal on the menu helped me make the right choices. The Turkey sandwich was served on some of the freshed bread I had sampled since my last visit to a bakery! Fresh greens, avocado and tomatoes made the sandwich light and fresh tasting. The small side quinoa and kale salad was fresh and light, complimented the soup and sandwich. As my eyes moved over to the fresh baked goods, Janyne helped me convince myself I should order the Reeses Peanut Butter cookie I had my eye on. As a hint, stop with one cookie, they are not small. To make things even better, Paradise Tropical tea is one of my favorite teas, crisp and fruity, must have been made fresh just before my arrival. I chose to sit outdoors and enjoy our cool weather, stepping outside reminded me of sitting outside at a winery in Paso Robles, which just happens to sit in the middle of an industrial area. Will I return? Of course I will!</Review><pictures>None<//pictures><Response>None< /Response>< Gmap_id>

< Text>
What works at a State Fair does not translate into good eats . So, let's start off with the Pull pork sandwich, the only taste was the BBQ sauce, bread was soggy , the cucumber salad with tomatoes. It needs something else..just a plain Jane,  the large basket with chicken, ribs, and rice, corn. The chicken had good flavor, well cooked, rice was perfect... the corn is questionable (hey.. why not try sweet corn?  It's a better fit for the combo meal)  The ribs were a catastrophe, sure they fall off the bone,  with zero flavors,  zero texture, zero excitement.  So  over cooked. (shaking my head).. Why Charlie, why?<//Text>

< text>
This location is located in a shopping mall and we were greeted quickly when we came in. They definitely have a different take on fast food which is neat and there is an assortment of items on the menu, but the items we ordered came out short on flavor.  We ordered the chicken breast sandwich , the chicken and waffles and the half rotisserie with tater tots. The food came quick and great looking but there was no flavor in any of the meals other than the sauce that was provided. It tasted as if it was cooked and served with no seasoning. Considering some of the other reviews maybe we just got a bad batch, so I'm willing to give it another shot.</text>

<Rate>4<//Rate>< text>
I was in San Diego for the Airshow and wanted chicken strip. Google maps is my go to, when I'm visiting another city. My first choice of establishment for chicken had a wait outside and Chicken Charlie's FRYBQ was listed next as closes distance from my original chicken restaurant. Therefore, I drove over and the establishment was clean, nice customer service, location was safe and appealing. I ordered the chicken tender basket and it was good. Chicken was not as tender as, I expected, but it was good. Also, the order came out really quick and was cooked. The chicken or fries had not been sitting under a heat lamp.
In addition, prices are reasonable and portion size is filling.

Thank you!</text>

<name>Jay Keyes<//name><Pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMWrSK6mH4KSa8ccQ4ks8MuzxJLiG7Y9iHrvOPS=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNiMpc-I729oDrTMRUIlK9SnSdcKSgmklWxf73o=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOYJHlhZQsR7mTtHL9kEbf0sq_RNtfgjh30mSsJ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /Pictures>< Text>
Chicken Charlie's served me the very worst food I've had in San Diego in the five years I've lived here.

I ordered the 2 piece Chicken Meal with Mashed Potatoes ($6.95) with a pint of beer. Thank goodness for the beer. I'm not exaggerating, the chicken was bone-dry. I knew I was in trouble when they brought the chicken out a minute after I ordered. How long had this been sitting under a lamp? Beyond the dryness, the chicken had an extremely salty, thin crust. No herbs or spices beyond burnt black pepper and salt -- LOTS of salt. The thin texture of the fried batter was similar to KFC's Original Recipe. Make no mistake though, the Colonel is like Escoffier next to Chicken Charlie. Chicken Charlie's fried chicken was fried in overworked rancid oil that may not have been changed since before I was born which, combined with the over-cooked meat and brutal onslaught of salt, made this one of the worst things I ever ate.

But WAIT... there's more! I haven't yet mentioned the mashed potatoes and gravy, WHICH WERE MADE WITH SPOILED DAIRY AND TASTED RANCID!

The food at this restaurant is horrible, a true single star experience.<//Text>

<Date>1500441748332< /Date><rating>4</rating><text>I came in here on July 15, 2017, at around 18:45 (6:45pm) with 3 of my friends. It was my first time here as well as one of my friends so we took a little longer to decide. The cashier (Vanessa according to receipt) was patient with us. I ordered the surf & turf burrito while my friend ordered the philly cheese sandwich, a loaded tots (I think it had pork in it), and my other friend was not hungry so he ordered sides which were tots and mash potato. I don't know how much it cost because my friend covered it, but I would estimate around $50. She gave us a number to put since it was for here.
We were about to sit outside, but realized that we wanted the nice A/C on the inside. Unfortunately, the only table available for 4 that I found was the one that was dirty. There was a water spill on the floor before I sat, which belong to the messy eater before us (just so you workers know that it was not me or my friends). Anyways, we were okay with it and I wiped the tables with the napkins. I worked at a fast food before (Jack in the Box) and I know that it is just timing. I am not going to complain about it since we want that spot.
Anyways, we sat down and waited for about 7-10 minutes for our food. After getting it, I ate my burrito, my friends ate their meal and I was not full. So I decided to go up and make a second round of order. My friend wanted the Oreo dessert. I was only going to order a side item, but realized that it was a few more dollars to get a little more so I decided to order a 2 piece chicken with onion rings as my side. After the cashier (this time Juan Carlos) rung my order, it was almost $11. The lady who brought the order to us asked if I wanted any sauce. I asked for a ranch sauce since I had onion rings. My friend was like "why you make her do work?" I realized he made that comment because she was pregnant (congrats btw) so I am sorry to ask for a ranch sauce. After eating my second round of meal I was not full, only satisfied. My friends were full. And that includes me eating a fried oreo. I do not know why I was not full at that night though since I did not do any physical exercises that day. But you can say that we left happy. Anyways, that is my food story of the night.
Now for the food, I want to mention that I liked the surf and turf a lot. The shrimp and steak was great. The french fries were crispy and the avocado made it all taste good to me. I also tried the loaded tots and I liked the flavoring of the bbq with the tots. I did not try my friend's philly cheese, but he said it was good. All my friends approve of the food. My second round of chicken was great too, it was not dry and the onion rings taste good. The fried oreo I had was perfect, it was not even that sweet.
Now, even though it was good, it did taste a little plain/bland. I was able to taste the food, but I was not able to taste it completely. The other fact is that it is greasy (what do you expect when it is fried?), and a bit salty though (probably why they serve beer here). To help my taste buds, I used their hot sauce on the counter and the ranch (kind of watery). But it is not that bad though. The sauce and water helped compliment my food.
Service here was good. Vanessa did a good job of bringing our order and being patient with us. Juan Carlos also does a lot of work here, I saw him stock and cleaning trash too. Thank you for the hard work.
Pricing wise, I think it is a bit pricey compared to other places that serve similar items, but it is reasonable. I did eat a lot for myself. Mine cost close to $18, but I was very hungry. (Side note: I got a lot of stares from my friends and people alike because I am more on the skinny side with a big appetite)
TL;DR: Although the food was a bit plain and salty-ish, my friends and I enjoyed our food. The service here was great during my stay and the price is reasonable. I would highly recommend a try here and my friends have a future plan on returning here.< /text>< pictures>

Disappointed in the The taste of the food. I purchased a full rack of ribs price was okay. The price is higher than Phil's BBQ which I found to be superior to chicken Charlie's. But I've heard so much about chicken Charlie's over the years mostly relating to their location at the del Mar Fair. I found that that Charlie's ribs were dryer and not has tasty as Phil barbecue.
I also purchased a Philadelphia cheesesteak sandwich. I'm from Philly and to me I know what I like in a cheesesteak. I know some people will think this is a good steak sandwich but do you use the word Philly in it to me is a real mistake. There is a restaurant sandwich shop I believe the name is the Philadelphia steak sandwiches it's up near Miramar now. They had what I would call a realistic steak sandwich from Philly. The bun that they have used is superior to the bun that take and Charlie's used. So on the two items that I purchased I can find better chasing products to me in the surrounding area. < text>
So, we went in there yesterday for the ribs and shrimp special. The ribs were, meh. They weren't bad, but there are several places in town with better taste and quality at a similar price point. The fried shrimp were equally unremarkable. A little more seasoning would make a world of  difference. Now, the bacon wrapped shrimp!  OMG! If they were all I had ordered, this would be a five star review, no doubt. The bacon seals in the juices of the shrimp perfectly! Add the crispness and flavor of bacon! Well, we all know bacon makes everything better. The biggest let down of all was the funnel cake. Very, very dry. Even topped with ice cream and whipped cream, it was still very dry. They do top it with fresh strawberries, but they need to add strawberry syrup or something to combat the dryness of the cake. Staff are very nice, polite and accomodating. The atmosphere was enjoyable.</text>
